posted:Posted March 24, 2024
msg:We actually decided to stay here before going to Dali for the second time. We didn't know about this hotel when we went to Dali for the first time. We just went to their restaurant and had a meal and fell in love with the overall design of their home.

üå≥Environment introduction:
This hotel is located in a villa community called Haidongfangdian in Haidong Town, east of Erhai Lake. You need to register as soon as you enter the community, so the security should be pretty good and at least a record will be left. The overall color and a**osphere has a Middle Eastern and Arabic feel, and there are plantings at the door. There are a lot of cacti and they are all very good varieties.

When we arrived, the building next to it was still being renovated. There would be some noise during the day, but the impact was not big. You need to go down the stairs to enter the lobby. As soon as you enter the lobby, you feel very relaxed. There is a large pool with a high-end feel outside the living room. Their cat is very cute, but she will scratch people if you don't touch her.

üè†Layout/room type:
After checking in, we will be introduced to the room. This time, we were upgraded to room No. 7 and room 8. The size of the two rooms is room 7, which is larger. The toilet is also very large and comfortable, but because room 7 The balcony is relatively deep, so the lighting in the room is relatively average.

Room No. 8 is a little small, but the lighting is surprisingly good. The whole room is bathed in the sunshine of Dali. You can lie on the sofa to bask in the sun and read a book, or you can lie on the chair on the balcony to bask in the sun. Basking in the sun and drinking drinks are great enjoyment.

The layout of the entire hotel on the east side is very comfortable and every corner can be seen to have been taken care of with care. It can be said that many Internet celebrity hotels or B&Bs often have an attractive place, such as a certain camera angle. Or maybe one of their locations is great, but at Liuyue I personally feel that films can be produced at every corner.

Of course, it will also have particularly classic locations or photo angles that you must try. And if you pay a little attention, every corner of the hotel can become a place for you to take photos.

üíÅFacility services:
They have a 24-hour butler service. Whenever you have any needs, you can tell them and they will usually meet your needs well. If they cannot be met, they will help you find ways to meet your needs as much as possible. All food and drink can be delivered to the room, and there is also good night sweet soup every night, which is different every day.

Breakfast is a semi-buffet with Chinese and Western options. The buffet items include bread, toast, fruits, freshly squeezed juices, and some steamed snacks. The Chinese style is Yunnan rice noodles. If you don't like rice noodles, you can ask for noodles. The portion is still very filling for a grown man like me.

üèùTIPS for surrounding travel:
Erhai Lake is right in front of you, so you can go for a walk around Erhai Lake, rent a bicycle or an electric bicycle and ride leisurely on Erhai Lake. Erhai Lake is also a good choice. If you drive nearby, you can go to Wenbi Village, Xiaoputuo, and Shuanglang Ancient Town, which are not very far away. . If you want to go to Dali city, it is very close by car. You can go shopping in shopping malls and eat to feel the urban a**osphere.
